## 1. Overview

The deliberation platform supports two modes of participation:

1. **Canonical Discourse**: Formal dialogue moves, structured arguments, and claims that become part of the official deliberation record
2. **Non-Canonical Participation**: Community contributions that require approval before becoming canonical

This document describes the systems that bridge informal community participation with formal deliberation structures.

### System Purposes

| System | Purpose | Approval Required |
|--------|---------|-------------------|
| **Propositions** | Informal discussion, voting, replies | No (direct participation) |
| **Issues** | Track questions, problems, moderation needs | Varies by kind |
| **Clarification Requests** | Ask authors to clarify their arguments | Author answers |
| **Non-Canonical Moves** | Community defense responses to arguments | Author approval |
| **CQ Responses** | Community answers to critical questions | Author selects canonical |

```
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ cq/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ CriticalQuestionsV2.tsx     # CQ management panel
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ CQStatusBadge.tsx           # Status visualization
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ CQResponseCard.tsx          # Individual response display
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ GroundsDefensePanel.tsx     # Author's CQ management
â”‚
â””â”€â”€ ncm/
    â”œâ”€â”€ NCMSubmissionForm.tsx       # Submit NCM
    â”œâ”€â”€ NCMExecutor.tsx             # Execute approved NCM
    â””â”€â”€ CommunityDefenseMenu.tsx    # Defense options menu
```

---

## 3. Non-Canonical Moves (NCM) System

### Overview

Non-Canonical Moves allow community members to contribute responses to arguments they didn't author. These contributions require author approval before becoming part of the canonical dialogue.

### Move Types

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```


### NCM Data Structure

```typescript
interface NonCanonicalMove {
  id: string;
  deliberationId: string;
  
  // Target of the response
  targetMoveId: string | null;     // Related dialogue move
  targetType: "argument" | "claim" | "clarification_request";
  targetId: string;
  
  // Participants
  contributorId: string;           // Who submitted
  authorId: string;                // Original author (approver)
  
  // Content
  moveType: MoveType;
  content: NCMContent;             // Move-specific payload
  
  // Status tracking
  status: NCMStatus;               // PENDING | APPROVED | EXECUTED | REJECTED | WITHDRAWN
  approvedBy: string | null;
  approvedAt: Date | null;
  rejectedBy: string | null;
  rejectedAt: Date | null;
  rejectionReason: string | null;
  
  // Execution
  canonicalMoveId: string | null;  // Links to DialogueMove when executed
  executedAt: Date | null;
  
  // Review tracking
  reviewIssues: Issue[];           // Linked issues for review workflow
}

interface NCMContent {
  text: string;
  citations?: Citation[];
  evidenceClaimIds?: string[];
  sourceUrls?: string[];
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
}
```


### NCM Executor Component

The `NCMExecutor` converts an approved NCM into a canonical DialogueMove:

```typescript
// NCMExecutor.tsx - Key Logic
async function executeNCM(ncmId: string): Promise<DialogueMove> {
  const ncm = await fetchNCM(ncmId);
  
  // 1. Create the dialogue move
  const dialogueMove = await createDialogueMove({
    deliberationId: ncm.deliberationId,
    authorId: ncm.contributorId,  // Community member becomes author
    moveType: mapNCMTypeToDialogueType(ncm.moveType),
    content: ncm.content,
    parentMoveId: ncm.targetMoveId,
    sourceNCMId: ncm.id,  // Provenance tracking
  });
  
  // 2. Update NCM status
  await updateNCM(ncmId, {
    status: "EXECUTED",
    canonicalMoveId: dialogueMove.id,
    executedAt: new Date(),
  });
  
  // 3. Close the review issue
  const issue = await findIssueByNCMId(ncmId);
  if (issue) {
    await closeIssue(issue.id, {
      resolution: "approved",
      note: `Executed as dialogue move ${dialogueMove.id}`,
    });
  }
  
  return dialogueMove;
}
```

---

## 4. Issues System

### Overview

The Issues system provides a unified workflow for tracking and resolving various types of review items, questions, and problems within a deliberation.

### Issue Kinds


### Issue Data Structure

```typescript
interface Issue {
  id: string;
  deliberationId: string;
  
  // Core fields
  label: string;
  description: string | null;
  state: "open" | "closed";
  kind: IssueKind;
  key: string | null;           // e.g., CQ key for CQ issues
  
  // Participants
  createdById: string;
  assigneeId: string | null;
  
  // Clarification-specific
  questionText: string | null;
  answerText: string | null;
  answeredAt: Date | null;
  answeredById: string | null;
  
  // NCM review-specific
  ncmId: string | null;
  ncmStatus: NCMStatus | null;
  reviewedAt: Date | null;
  reviewNotes: string | null;
  
  // Relationships
  links: IssueLink[];
  
  // Timestamps
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

interface IssueLink {
  issueId: string;
  targetType: "argument" | "claim" | "card" | "inference";
  targetId: string;
  role: "related" | "source" | "target" | null;
}
```

## 5. Critical Questions (CQ) Response System

### Overview

Critical Questions are scheme-specific challenges that test the validity of an argument. The CQ Response system allows community members to provide answers to these questions, with the original author selecting which response becomes canonical.

### CQ Status Lifecycle

```

           â”‚ SATISFIED  â”‚ â”‚ (canonical â”‚ â”‚ (conflict â”‚
           â”‚ (weak      â”‚ â”‚  response  â”‚ â”‚  between  â”‚
           â”‚  answer)   â”‚ â”‚  selected) â”‚ â”‚  answers) â”‚
           â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜ â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜ â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### CQ Data Structures

```typescript
interface CQStatus {
  id: string;
  
  // Target identification
  targetType: "claim" | "argument";
  targetId: string;
  argumentId: string | null;
  
  // CQ identification
  schemeKey: string;            // e.g., "EXPERT_OPINION"
  cqKey: string;                // e.g., "CQ1", "CQ2"
  
  // Status tracking
  statusEnum: CQStatusEnum;     // OPEN | PENDING_REVIEW | PARTIALLY_SATISFIED | SATISFIED | DISPUTED
  
  // Canonical response
  canonicalResponseId: string | null;
  
  // Relationships
  responses: CQResponse[];
  activities: CQActivityLog[];
  attacks: CQAttack[];
}

interface CQResponse {
  id: string;
  cqStatusId: string;
  
  // Response content
  groundsText: string;
  evidenceClaimIds: string[];
  sourceUrls: string[];
  
  // Approval tracking
  responseStatus: ResponseStatus;  // PENDING | APPROVED | CANONICAL | REJECTED | SUPERSEDED | WITHDRAWN
  
  // Attribution
  contributorId: string;
  
  // Community feedback
  upvotes: number;
  downvotes: number;
  
  // Timestamps
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

enum ResponseStatus {
  PENDING,      // Awaiting review
  APPROVED,     // Accepted as valid
  CANONICAL,    // Selected as the definitive answer
  REJECTED,     // Not accepted
  SUPERSEDED,   // Replaced by better answer
  WITHDRAWN     // Contributor withdrew
}
```

### CQ-to-Attack Type Mapping

Each critical question, when answered negatively, generates a specific type of attack:


### CQ Component: CriticalQuestionsV2


### CQ Response Voting

Community members can vote on responses to surface the best answers:

```typescript
// Vote on CQ Response
POST /api/cq/responses/{id}/vote
{
  value: 1   // 1 = upvote, -1 = downvote
}

// Response updates
{
  upvotes: 6,
  downvotes: 1,
  userVote: 1  // Current user's vote
}
```

### CQ as Virtual Attacker

Unanswered critical questions can be visualized as "virtual attackers" on an argument:


## 6. Clarification Requests

### Overview

Clarification requests allow community members to ask authors to explain or clarify aspects of their arguments. They are implemented as a special kind of Issue (`kind: "clarification"`).

### Clarification Request Flow

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

## 7. Propositions System

### Overview

Propositions provide an informal discussion layer where community members can share ideas, vote on content, and engage in threaded replies. Unlike formal arguments, propositions don't require structured premises or schemes.

### Proposition Lifecycle

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

### Proposition Data Structure

```typescript
interface Proposition {
  id: string;
  deliberationId: string;
  authorId: string;
  
  // Content
  text: string;
  mediaType: "text" | "image" | "video" | "audio";
  mediaUrl: string | null;
  
  // Status
  status: PropositionStatus;  // DRAFT | PUBLISHED | CLAIMED | ARCHIVED
  
  // Promotion to formal claim
  promotedClaimId: string | null;
  promotedClaim: Claim | null;
  
  // Engagement counters (denormalized for performance)
  voteUpCount: number;
  voteDownCount: number;
  endorseCount: number;
  replyCount: number;
  
  // Relationships
  votes: PropositionVote[];
  endorsements: PropositionEndorsement[];
  replies: PropositionReply[];
  tags: PropositionTag[];
  
  // Timestamps
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

interface PropositionVote {
  propositionId: string;
  userId: string;
  value: -1 | 0 | 1;  // -1 = downvote, 0 = neutral, 1 = upvote
  createdAt: Date;
}

interface PropositionReply {
  id: string;
  propositionId: string;
  authorId: string;
  text: string;
  parentReplyId: string | null;  // For nested threading
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

interface PropositionEndorsement {
  propositionId: string;
  userId: string;
  createdAt: Date;
}
```

### PropositionsList Component


## 9. API Routes Reference

### Issues API

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose | Key Parameters |
|----------|--------|---------|----------------|
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues` | GET | List issues | `state`, `kind`, `search`, `argumentId` |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues` | POST | Create issue | `label`, `kind`, `targets`, `questionText` |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues/[issueId]` | GET | Get issue details | - |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues/[issueId]` | PATCH | Update issue | `state`, `assigneeId`, `description` |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues/[issueId]` | DELETE | Delete issue | - |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues/[issueId]/answer` | POST | Submit clarification answer | `answerText` |
| `/api/deliberations/[id]/issues/counts` | GET | Get issue counts by kind | - |

### NCM API

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose | Key Parameters |
|----------|--------|---------|----------------|
| `/api/ncm` | POST | Submit NCM | `targetId`, `targetType`, `moveType`, `content` |
| `/api/ncm/[id]` | GET | Get NCM details | - |
| `/api/ncm/[id]/approve` | POST | Approve NCM | - |
| `/api/ncm/[id]/reject` | POST | Reject NCM | `rejectionReason` |
| `/api/ncm/[id]/execute` | POST | Execute approved NCM | - |
| `/api/ncm/[id]/withdraw` | POST | Withdraw NCM | - |

### CQ Response API

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose | Key Parameters |
|----------|--------|---------|----------------|
| `/api/cq/status` | GET | Get CQ status for target | `targetType`, `targetId` |
| `/api/cq/responses` | POST | Submit CQ response | `cqStatusId`, `groundsText`, `evidenceClaimIds` |
| `/api/cq/responses/[id]` | GET | Get response details | - |
| `/api/cq/responses/[id]/vote` | POST | Vote on response | `value` (-1, 0, 1) |
| `/api/cq/responses/[id]/approve` | POST | Approve response | - |
| `/api/cq/responses/[id]/canonical` | POST | Set as canonical | - |
| `/api/cq/responses/[id]/reject` | POST | Reject response | `reason` |

### Propositions API

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose | Key Parameters |
|----------|--------|---------|----------------|
| `/api/propositions` | GET | List propositions | `deliberationId`, `sort`, `filter`, `page` |
| `/api/propositions` | POST | Create proposition | `text`, `deliberationId`, `tags` |
| `/api/propositions/[id]` | GET | Get proposition | - |
| `/api/propositions/[id]` | PATCH | Update proposition | `text`, `status` |
| `/api/propositions/[id]` | DELETE | Delete proposition | - |
| `/api/propositions/[id]/vote` | POST | Vote on proposition | `value` (-1, 0, 1) |
| `/api/propositions/[id]/endorse` | POST | Endorse proposition | - |
| `/api/propositions/[id]/replies` | GET | Get replies | `page` |
| `/api/propositions/[id]/replies` | POST | Add reply | `text`, `parentReplyId` |
| `/api/propositions/[id]/promote` | POST | Promote to claim | `claimText` |

---

```
     â”‚                 â”‚                  â”‚                  â”‚               â”‚
     â”‚                 â”‚                  â”‚                  â”‚ 9. Refresh    â”‚
     â”‚                 â”‚                  â”‚                  â”‚ CQ meter      â”‚

     â”‚                 â”‚                  â”‚                  â”‚ 10. Remove    â”‚
```

## 11. Database Schema

### Core Models

```prisma
// ============================================================================
// NON-CANONICAL MOVES
// ============================================================================

model NonCanonicalMove {
  id              String    @id @default(cuid())
  deliberationId  String
  
  // Target of the response
  targetMoveId    String?   // Related dialogue move
  targetType      String    // "argument" | "claim" | "clarification_request"
  targetId        String
  
  // Participants
  contributorId   String    // User who submitted
  authorId        String    // Original author (for approval)
  
  // Content
  moveType        MoveType
  content         Json      // Move-specific payload
  
  // Status tracking
  status          NCMStatus @default(PENDING)
  approvedBy      String?
  approvedAt      DateTime?
  rejectedBy      String?
  rejectedAt      DateTime?
  rejectionReason String?
  
  // Execution
  canonicalMoveId String?   @unique
  executedAt      DateTime?
  
  // Relationships
  reviewIssues    Issue[]
  
  createdAt       DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime  @updatedAt
  
  @@map("non_canonical_moves")
}

enum NCMStatus {
  PENDING
  APPROVED
  EXECUTED
  REJECTED
  WITHDRAWN
}

enum MoveType {
  GROUNDS_RESPONSE
  CLARIFICATION_ANSWER
  CHALLENGE_RESPONSE
  EVIDENCE_ADDITION
  PREMISE_DEFENSE
  EXCEPTION_REBUTTAL
}

// ============================================================================
// ISSUES
// ============================================================================

model Issue {
  id              String      @id @default(cuid())
  deliberationId  String
  
  // Core fields
  label           String
  description     String?
  state           IssueState  @default(open)
  kind            IssueKind   @default(general)
  key             String?     // e.g., CQ key
  
  // Participants
  createdById     BigInt
  assigneeId      BigInt?
  
  // Clarification-specific
  questionText    String?
  answerText      String?
  answeredAt      DateTime?
  answeredById    BigInt?
  
  // NCM review-specific
  ncmId           String?
  ncmStatus       NCMStatus?
  reviewedAt      DateTime?
  reviewNotes     String?
  
  // Relationships
  links           IssueLink[]
  ncm             NonCanonicalMove? @relation(fields: [ncmId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt       DateTime    @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime    @updatedAt
  
  @@map("issues")
}

enum IssueState {
  open
  closed
}

enum IssueKind {
  general
  cq
  moderation
  evidence
  structural
  governance
  clarification
  community_defense
}

model IssueLink {
  id          String              @id @default(cuid())
  issueId     String
  targetType  IssueLinkTargetType
  targetId    String
  role        IssueLinkRole?
  
  issue       Issue               @relation(fields: [issueId], references: [id])
  
  @@unique([issueId, targetType, targetId])
  @@map("issue_links")
}

enum IssueLinkTargetType {
  argument
  claim
  card
  inference
}

enum IssueLinkRole {
  related
  source
  target
}

// ============================================================================
// CRITICAL QUESTIONS
// ============================================================================

model CQStatus {
  id                  String        @id @default(cuid())
  
  // Target
  targetType          TargetType
  targetId            String
  argumentId          String?
  
  // CQ identification
  schemeKey           String
  cqKey               String
  
  // Status
  statusEnum          CQStatusEnum  @default(OPEN)
  canonicalResponseId String?
  
  // Relationships
  responses           CQResponse[]
  activities          CQActivityLog[]
  attacks             CQAttack[]
  
  createdAt           DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt           DateTime      @updatedAt
  
  @@unique([targetType, targetId, schemeKey, cqKey])
  @@map("cq_status")
}

enum TargetType {
  claim
  argument
}

enum CQStatusEnum {
  OPEN
  PENDING_REVIEW
  PARTIALLY_SATISFIED
  SATISFIED
  DISPUTED
}

model CQResponse {
  id              String          @id @default(cuid())
  cqStatusId      String
  
  // Content
  groundsText     String
  evidenceClaimIds String[]
  sourceUrls      String[]
  
  // Status
  responseStatus  ResponseStatus  @default(PENDING)
  
  // Attribution
  contributorId   String
  
  // Voting
  upvotes         Int             @default(0)
  downvotes       Int             @default(0)
  
  // Relationships
  cqStatus        CQStatus        @relation(fields: [cqStatusId], references: [id])
  votes           CQResponseVote[]
  
  createdAt       DateTime        @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime        @updatedAt
  
  @@map("cq_responses")
}

enum ResponseStatus {
  PENDING
  APPROVED
  CANONICAL
  REJECTED
  SUPERSEDED
  WITHDRAWN
}

model CQResponseVote {
  id            String      @id @default(cuid())
  responseId    String
  userId        String
  value         Int         // -1 or 1
  
  response      CQResponse  @relation(fields: [responseId], references: [id])
  
  @@unique([responseId, userId])
  @@map("cq_response_votes")
}

// ============================================================================
// PROPOSITIONS
// ============================================================================

model Proposition {
  id              String              @id @default(cuid())
  deliberationId  String
  authorId        String
  
  // Content
  text            String
  mediaType       String              @default("text")
  mediaUrl        String?
  
  // Status
  status          PropositionStatus   @default(PUBLISHED)
  
  // Promotion
  promotedClaimId String?             @unique
  promotedClaim   Claim?              @relation("PropositionClaim", fields: [promotedClaimId], references: [id])
  
  // Counters (denormalized)
  voteUpCount     Int                 @default(0)
  voteDownCount   Int                 @default(0)
  endorseCount    Int                 @default(0)
  replyCount      Int                 @default(0)
  
  // Relationships
  votes           PropositionVote[]
  endorsements    PropositionEndorsement[]
  replies         PropositionReply[]
  tags            PropositionTag[]
  
  createdAt       DateTime            @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime            @updatedAt
  
  @@map("propositions")
}

enum PropositionStatus {
  DRAFT
  PUBLISHED
  CLAIMED
  ARCHIVED
}

model PropositionVote {
  propositionId String
  userId        String
  value         Int           // -1, 0, 1
  
  proposition   Proposition   @relation(fields: [propositionId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt     DateTime      @default(now())
  
  @@id([propositionId, userId])
  @@map("proposition_votes")
}

model PropositionReply {
  id            String        @id @default(cuid())
  propositionId String
  authorId      String
  text          String
  parentReplyId String?       // For nested threading
  
  proposition   Proposition   @relation(fields: [propositionId], references: [id])
  parent        PropositionReply?  @relation("ReplyThread", fields: [parentReplyId], references: [id])
  children      PropositionReply[] @relation("ReplyThread")
  
  createdAt     DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime      @updatedAt
  
  @@index([propositionId, createdAt])
  @@map("proposition_replies")
}

model PropositionEndorsement {
  propositionId String
  userId        String
  
  proposition   Proposition   @relation(fields: [propositionId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt     DateTime      @default(now())
  
  @@id([propositionId, userId])
  @@map("proposition_endorsements")
}

model PropositionTag {
  id            String        @id @default(cuid())
  propositionId String
  tag           String
  
  proposition   Proposition   @relation(fields: [propositionId], references: [id])
  
  @@unique([propositionId, tag])
  @@map("proposition_tags")
}
```

---

## 12. Summary

This document describes the community participation systems that bridge informal discussion with formal deliberation:

### System Overview

| System | Purpose | Approval Flow | Outcome |
|--------|---------|---------------|---------|
| **NCM** | Community defense of arguments | Author approves/rejects | Becomes DialogueMove |
| **Issues** | Track review items and questions | Varies by kind | Resolution or closure |
| **CQ Responses** | Answer critical questions | Author selects canonical | CQ marked satisfied |
| **Clarifications** | Ask for explanation | Author answers | Answer stored in Issue |
| **Propositions** | Informal discussion | Direct voting | Optional promotion to Claim |

### Key Design Patterns

1. **Author Sovereignty**: Original authors control what becomes canonical
2. **Community Contribution**: Anyone can propose, vote, and participate
3. **Issue Tracking**: All review workflows tracked as Issues
4. **Informal â†’ Formal Pipeline**: Clear path from discussion to deliberation

### Component Summary

| Component | Location | Purpose |
|-----------|----------|---------|
| `IssuesList` | `components/issues/` | View and filter issues |
| `IssueDetail` | `components/issues/` | Review and resolve issues |
| `NCMReviewCard` | `components/issues/` | Approve/reject NCMs |
| `CriticalQuestionsV2` | `components/cq/` | Manage CQ responses |
| `PropositionsList` | `components/propositions/` | Browse propositions |
| `PropositionComposerPro` | `components/propositions/` | Create rich propositions |

---
